# atl command reference

This file is generated by `scripts/gen-docs.sh` from the clap command tree. Do not edit by hand.

## atl

Unified CLI for Atlassian Confluence and Jira

**Usage**

```
Usage: atl [OPTIONS] <COMMAND>
```

**Options**

- `--verbose, -v` — Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` — Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` — Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` — Profile name to use
- `--format, -F` — Output format
- `--no-color` — Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` — Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` — Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` — Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` — Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)
- `--retry-all-methods` — Retry all HTTP methods, not just GET/HEAD/OPTIONS. May cause duplicate writes on transient failures (a POST that creates a resource may run twice)

**Subcommands**

- `confluence` — Confluence operations
- `jira` — Jira operations
- `init` — Initialize configuration file
- `config` — Manage configuration profiles
- `completions` — Generate shell completion scripts
- `self` — Manage the atl binary itself (check/update)
- `api` — Make an authenticated REST request against Confluence or Jira
- `browse` — Open a Confluence page or Jira issue in the default browser
- `alias` — Manage user-defined command aliases
- `auth` — Manage authentication — login, logout, status, token

### atl confluence

Confluence operations

**Usage**

```
Usage: atl confluence [OPTIONS] <COMMAND>
```

**Options**

- `--verbose, -v` — Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` — Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` — Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` — Profile name to use
- `--format, -F` — Output format
- `--no-color` — Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` — Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` — Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` — Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` — Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)
- `--retry-all-methods` — Retry all HTTP methods, not just GET/HEAD/OPTIONS. May cause duplicate writes on transient failures (a POST that creates a resource may run twice)

**Subcommands**

- `read` — Read a page by ID
- `info` — Get page metadata
- `search` — Search pages with CQL
- `space` — List spaces
- `children` — List child pages
- `create` — Create a new page
- `update` — Update an existing page
- `delete` — Delete a page
- `attachment` — Attachment operations
- `find` — Find pages by title
- `export` — Export a page with attachments to a local directory
- `copy-tree` — Copy a page tree to another space/parent
- `property` — Content property operations
- `label` — Label management
- `blog` — Blog post management
- `versions` — Page version history
- `version-detail` — Get a specific page version
- `likes` — Page likes
- `operations` — Page operations/permissions
- `ancestors` — Page ancestors
- `descendants` — Page descendants
- `footer-comment` — Footer comment management (v2)
- `inline-comment` — Inline comment management (v2)
- `whiteboard` — Whiteboard management
- `database` — Database management
- `folder` — Folder management
- `custom-content` — Custom content management
- `task` — Task management
- `admin-key` — Admin key management
- `classification` — Content classification management
- `user` — Confluence user operations
- `convert-ids` — Convert content IDs between formats
- `app-property` — App property management
- `page-list` — List pages (v2)
- `update-title` — Update page title only
- `likes-count` — Get like count for a page
- `likes-users` — Get users who liked a page
- `page-custom-content` — List custom content in a page
- `redact` — Redact content from a page

#### atl confluence read

Read a page by ID

**Usage**

```
Usage: atl confluence read [OPTIONS] <PAGE_ID>
```

**Options**

- `<PAGE_ID>` — Page ID
- `--body-format` — Body format
- `--no-directives` — Strip MyST-style directives (`:::info`/`:::warning`/etc.) from markdown output. No effect when `--body-format` is not `markdown`
- `--include-labels` — Include labels in the response
- `--include-properties` — Include properties in the response
- `--include-operations` — Include operations in the response
- `--include-versions` — Include version details in the response
- `--include-collaborators` — Include collaborators in the response
- `--include-favorited-by` — Include favorited-by info in the response
- `--web` — Open the page in a browser instead of printing
- `--verbose, -v` — Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` — Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` — Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` — Profile name to use
- `--format, -F` — Output format
- `--no-color` — Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` — Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` — Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` — Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` — Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)
- `--retry-all-methods` — Retry all HTTP methods, not just GET/HEAD/OPTIONS. May cause duplicate writes on transient failures (a POST that creates a resource may run twice)

#### atl confluence search

Search pages with CQL

**Usage**

```
Usage: atl confluence search [OPTIONS] <CQL>
```

**Options**

- `<CQL>` — CQL query
- `--limit, -l` — Max results per page
- `--all` — Fetch all results (auto-paginate)
- `--verbose, -v` — Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` — Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` — Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` — Profile name to use

##### atl confluence space create

Create a space

**Usage**

```
Usage: atl confluence space create [OPTIONS] --key <KEY> --name <NAME>
```

**Options**

- `--key, -k` — Space key
- `--name, -n` — Space name
- `--description, -d` — Space description
- `--private` — Create as a private (personal) space
- `--alias` — Space alias
- `--template-key` — Template key to use for the space homepage
- `--verbose, -v` — Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` — Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` — Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` — Profile name to use

#### atl confluence create

Create a new page

**Usage**

```
Usage: atl confluence create [OPTIONS] --title <TITLE> --body <BODY>
```

**Options**

- `--space, -s` — Space key (resolved to ID internally)
- `--space-id` — Space ID (numeric, skips key-to-ID lookup)
- `--title, -t` — Page title
- `--body, -b` — Page body. Use @file to read from file, or - for stdin
- `--parent` — Parent page ID
- `--input-format` — Input format for the body
- `--private` — Create as a private (personal) page
- `--subtype` — Page subtype (e.g. "page", "blog")
- `--embedded` — Create as embedded content
- `--root-level` — Create at root level (no parent)
- `--verbose, -v` — Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` — Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` — Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` — Profile name to use
- `--format, -F` — Output format
- `--no-color` — Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` — Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` — Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` — Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` — Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)
- `--retry-all-methods` — Retry all HTTP methods, not just GET/HEAD/OPTIONS. May cause duplicate writes on transient failures (a POST that creates a resource may run twice)

#### atl confluence copy-tree

Copy a page tree to another space/parent

**Usage**

```
Usage: atl confluence copy-tree [OPTIONS] <SOURCE_PAGE_ID>
```

**Options**

- `<SOURCE_PAGE_ID>` — Source page ID (root of the tree to copy)
- `--target-space` — Target space key (resolved to ID internally)
- `--target-space-id` — Target space ID (numeric, skips key-to-ID lookup)
- `--target-parent` — Target parent page ID
- `--depth, -d` — Maximum depth to copy (0 = source page only)
- `--dry-run` — Show what would be copied without making changes
- `--exclude` — Glob pattern to exclude pages by title
- `--verbose, -v` — Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` — Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` — Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` — Profile name to use
- `--format, -F` — Output format
- `--no-color` — Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` — Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` — Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` — Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` — Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)
- `--retry-all-methods` — Retry all HTTP methods, not just GET/HEAD/OPTIONS. May cause duplicate writes on transient failures (a POST that creates a resource may run twice)

##### atl confluence blog read

```

- `<BLOG_ID>` — Blog post ID

- `--include-labels` — Include labels in the response
- `--include-properties` — Include properties in the response
- `--include-operations` — Include operations in the response
- `--include-versions` — Include version details in the response
- `--include-collaborators` — Include collaborators in the response

- `--quiet, -q` — Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` — Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` — Profile name to use
- `--format, -F` — Output format
- `--no-color` — Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` — Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` — Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` — Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` — Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)
- `--retry-all-methods` — Retry all HTTP methods, not just GET/HEAD/OPTIONS. May cause duplicate writes on transient failures (a POST that creates a resource may run twice)

```
Usage: atl confluence inline-comment [OPTIONS] <COMMAND>
```

**Options**

- `--verbose, -v` — Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` — Suppress all output except errors

- `--inline-marker-ref` — Inline marker reference (from the page content)
- `--text-selection` — Text selection to highlight
- `--verbose, -v` — Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` — Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` — Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` — Profile name to use

- `--verbose, -v` — Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` — Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` — Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` — Profile name to use
- `--format, -F` — Output format
- `--no-color` — Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` — Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` — Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` — Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` — Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)
- `--retry-all-methods` — Retry all HTTP methods, not just GET/HEAD/OPTIONS. May cause duplicate writes on transient failures (a POST that creates a resource may run twice)

- `--config` — Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` — Profile name to use
- `--format, -F` — Output format
- `--no-color` — Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` — Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` — Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` — Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` — Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)
- `--retry-all-methods` — Retry all HTTP methods, not just GET/HEAD/OPTIONS. May cause duplicate writes on transient failures (a POST that creates a resource may run twice)

**Subcommands**

- `create` — Create
- `get` — Get by ID
- `delete` — Delete
- `ancestors` — List ancestors
- `descendants` — List descendants
- `children` — List direct children
- `operations` — List operations
- `property` — Content property operations

##### atl confluence folder create

```

**Options**

- `--space-id, -s` — Space ID
- `--title, -t` — Title
- `--template-key` — Template key (for whiteboards)
- `--parent-id` — Parent content ID

**Options**

- `--verbose, -v` — Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` — Suppress all output except errors

- `--content-type, -t` — Custom content type
- `--space-id, -s` — Space ID
- `--title` — Title
- `--body, -b` — Body. Use @file to read from file, or - for stdin
- `--verbose, -v` — Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` — Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` — Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` — Profile name to use

- `--no-color` — Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` — Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` — Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` — Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` — Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)
- `--retry-all-methods` — Retry all HTTP methods, not just GET/HEAD/OPTIONS. May cause duplicate writes on transient failures (a POST that creates a resource may run twice)

### atl jira

Jira operations

**Usage**

```
Usage: atl jira [OPTIONS] <COMMAND>
```

**Options**

- `--verbose, -v` — Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` — Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` — Path to configuration file

- `--format, -F` — Output format
- `--no-color` — Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` — Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` — Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` — Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` — Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)
- `--retry-all-methods` — Retry all HTTP methods, not just GET/HEAD/OPTIONS. May cause duplicate writes on transient failures (a POST that creates a resource may run twice)

**Subcommands**

- `search` — Search issues with JQL
- `view` — View an issue
- `create` — Create a new issue
- `update` — Update an issue
- `delete` — Delete an issue
- `move` — Transition an issue to another status
- `assign` — Assign an issue
- `comment` — Add a comment to an issue
- `comments` — List comments for an issue
- `comment-get` — Get a specific comment
- `comment-delete` — Delete a comment
- `transitions` — List available transitions for an issue
- `project` — Project management
- `board` — Board management
- `sprint` — Sprint management
- `backlog-move` — Move issues to backlog
- `me` — Show current user info
- `epic` — Epic management
- `link` — Link two issues
- `link-type` — Issue link type management
- `issue-link-get` — Get an issue link by ID
- `issue-link-delete` — Delete an issue link by ID
- `remote-link` — Add a remote link to an issue
- `remote-links` — List remote links for an issue
- `remote-link-delete` — Delete a remote link
- `clone` — Clone an issue
- `worklog` — Worklog management
- `filter` — Saved filter management
- `attach` — Attach a file to an issue
- `watch` — Watch an issue
- `unwatch` — Unwatch an issue
- `watchers` — List watchers for an issue
- `vote` — Vote for an issue
- `unvote` — Remove your vote from an issue
- `changelog` — View issue changelog (history of changes)
- `component` — Component management
- `version` — Version management
- `dashboard` — Dashboard management
- `field` — Field management
- `user` — User operations
- `group` — Group management
- `notify` — Send a notification about an issue
- `create-meta` — Get issue creation metadata
- `edit-meta` — Get issue edit metadata
- `issue-type` — Issue type management
- `priority` — Priority management
- `resolution` — Resolution management
- `status` — Status management
- `screen` — Screen management
- `workflow` — Workflow management
- `workflow-scheme` — Workflow scheme management
- `permission-scheme` — Permission scheme management
- `notification-scheme` — Notification scheme management
- `issue-security-scheme` — Issue security scheme management
- `field-config` — Field configuration management
- `issue-type-scheme` — Issue type scheme management
- `role` — Standalone role management
- `banner` — Announcement banner
- `configuration` — View system configuration
- `task` — Async task management
- `attachment` — Attachment administration
- `project-category` — Project category management
- `server-info` — Show server information
- `webhook` — Webhook management
- `audit-records` — View audit records
- `permissions` — List all permissions
- `my-permissions` — List my permissions
- `labels` — List all labels
- `bulk-create` — Bulk create issues from a JSON array
- `archive` — Archive one or more issues
- `unarchive` — Unarchive one or more issues

#### atl jira search

Search issues with JQL

**Usage**

```
Usage: atl jira search [OPTIONS] [JQL]
```

**Options**

- `<JQL>` — JQL query (combined with filter flags via AND)
- `--limit, -l` — Max results per page
- `--all` — Fetch all results (auto-paginate)
- `--fields, -f` — Fields to return (comma-separated)
- `--status` — Filter by status name (e.g. "Open", "In Progress")
- `--priority` — Filter by priority name
- `--assignee` — Filter by assignee (account ID or "currentUser()")
- `--reporter` — Filter by reporter
- `--type` — Filter by issue type (e.g. Bug, Task, Story)
- `--label` — Filter by label
- `--component` — Filter by component
- `--resolution` — Filter by resolution
- `--created` — Filter: created on or after date (YYYY-MM-DD)
- `--created-after` — Filter: created after date (YYYY-MM-DD)
- `--updated` — Filter: updated on or after date (YYYY-MM-DD)
- `--updated-after` — Filter: updated after date (YYYY-MM-DD)
- `--watching` — Only issues you are watching
- `--order-by` — Order results by field (e.g. "created", "priority")
- `--reverse` — Reverse sort order (use with --order-by)
- `--verbose, -v` — Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` — Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` — Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` — Profile name to use
- `--format, -F` — Output format
- `--no-color` — Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` — Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` — Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` — Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` — Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)
- `--retry-all-methods` — Retry all HTTP methods, not just GET/HEAD/OPTIONS. May cause duplicate writes on transient failures (a POST that creates a resource may run twice)

#### atl jira view

View an issue

**Usage**

```
Usage: atl jira view [OPTIONS] <KEY>
```

**Options**

- `<KEY>` — Issue key (e.g. PROJ-123)
- `--web` — Open the issue in a browser instead of printing
- `--body-format` — Output format for description and comment bodies
- `--no-directives` — Strip MyST-style directives (`:::info`/`:::warning`/etc.) from markdown output. No effect when `--body-format` is not `markdown`
- `--verbose, -v` — Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` — Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` — Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` — Profile name to use
- `--format, -F` — Output format
- `--no-color` — Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` — Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` — Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` — Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` — Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)
- `--retry-all-methods` — Retry all HTTP methods, not just GET/HEAD/OPTIONS. May cause duplicate writes on transient failures (a POST that creates a resource may run twice)

#### atl jira create

Create a new issue

**Usage**

```
Usage: atl jira create [OPTIONS] --project <PROJECT> --issue-type <ISSUE_TYPE> --summary <SUMMARY>
```

**Options**

- `--project` — Project key
- `--issue-type, -t` — Issue type (e.g. Task, Bug, Story)
- `--summary, -s` — Summary
- `--description, -d` — Description
- `--assignee` — Assignee account ID
- `--priority` — Priority name
- `--labels` — Labels (comma-separated)
- `--parent` — Parent issue key (for subtasks)
- `--fix-version` — Fix version(s), comma-separated
- `--component` — Component(s), comma-separated
- `--custom` — Custom field (repeatable), e.g. --custom customfield_10001=value
- `--input-format` — Input format for the body
- `--verbose, -v` — Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` — Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` — Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` — Profile name to use
- `--format, -F` — Output format
- `--no-color` — Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` — Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` — Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` — Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` — Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)
- `--retry-all-methods` — Retry all HTTP methods, not just GET/HEAD/OPTIONS. May cause duplicate writes on transient failures (a POST that creates a resource may run twice)

- `--transition, -t` — Transition ID
- `--verbose, -v` — Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` — Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` — Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` — Profile name to use
- `--format, -F` — Output format
- `--no-color` — Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` — Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` — Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` — Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` — Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)
- `--retry-all-methods` — Retry all HTTP methods, not just GET/HEAD/OPTIONS. May cause duplicate writes on transient failures (a POST that creates a resource may run twice)

- `--quiet, -q` — Suppress all output except errors

**Subcommands**

- `list` — List groups
- `get` — Get group details
- `create` — Create a group
- `delete` — Delete a group
- `members` — List group members
- `add-user` — Add a user to a group
- `remove-user` — Remove a user from a group
- `search` — Search groups

##### atl jira group list

List groups

**Usage**

```
Usage: atl jira group list [OPTIONS]
```

**Options**

- `--verbose, -v` — Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` — Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` — Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` — Profile name to use
- `--format, -F` — Output format
- `--no-color` — Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` — Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` — Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` — Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` — Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)
- `--retry-all-methods` — Retry all HTTP methods, not just GET/HEAD/OPTIONS. May cause duplicate writes on transient failures (a POST that creates a resource may run twice)

#### atl jira notify

Send a notification about an issue

**Usage**

```
Usage: atl jira notify [OPTIONS] --subject <SUBJECT> --body <BODY> <KEY>
```

**Options**

- `<KEY>` — Issue key (e.g. PROJ-123)
- `--subject, -s` — Notification subject
- `--body, -b` — Notification body. Use @file to read from file, or - for stdin
- `--to` — Recipient account IDs (repeatable)
- `--verbose, -v` — Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` — Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` — Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` — Profile name to use
- `--format, -F` — Output format
- `--no-color` — Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` — Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` — Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` — Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` — Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)
- `--retry-all-methods` — Retry all HTTP methods, not just GET/HEAD/OPTIONS. May cause duplicate writes on transient failures (a POST that creates a resource may run twice)

- `--message, -m` — Banner message (HTML)
- `--is-enabled` — Enable or disable the banner
- `--visibility` — Visibility: "public" or "private"
- `--verbose, -v` — Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` — Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` — Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` — Profile name to use
- `--format, -F` — Output format
- `--no-color` — Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` — Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` — Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` — Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` — Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)
- `--retry-all-methods` — Retry all HTTP methods, not just GET/HEAD/OPTIONS. May cause duplicate writes on transient failures (a POST that creates a resource may run twice)

- `--retry-all-methods` — Retry all HTTP methods, not just GET/HEAD/OPTIONS. May cause duplicate writes on transient failures (a POST that creates a resource may run twice)

Download and replace the current binary with the latest release

```

- `--to` — Install a specific version instead of latest (e.g. 2026.16.2)

- `--verbose, -v` — Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` — Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` — Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` — Profile name to use
- `--format, -F` — Output format

### atl api

Make an authenticated REST request against Confluence or Jira

**Usage**

```
Usage: atl api [OPTIONS] --service <SERVICE> <ENDPOINT>
```

**Options**

- `<ENDPOINT>` — REST endpoint path (e.g. `rest/api/2/myself`). Leading slash optional
- `--service` — Which Atlassian product to target
- `--method, -X` — HTTP method (default: GET)
- `--header, -H` — Custom header in the form `KEY:VALUE`. Repeatable
- `--field, -f` — String field in the JSON body, `KEY=VALUE`. `VALUE` may be `@file` to read the contents of a file, or `-` to read stdin. Repeatable. Mutually exclusive with `--input`
- `--raw-field` — Raw JSON field in the JSON body, `KEY=VALUE`. `VALUE` is parsed as JSON (e.g. `--raw-field count=42`, `--raw-field tags=[1,2,3]`). Repeatable. Mutually exclusive with `--input`. No short form because `-F` is reserved for `--format`
- `--input` — Read the request body verbatim from a file, or `-` for stdin. Mutually exclusive with `--field` / `--raw-field`
- `--query` — Query parameter in the form `KEY=VALUE`. Repeatable. No short form because `-q` is reserved for `--quiet`
- `--paginate` — Auto-follow pagination until the server reports no more pages
- `--max-pages` — Maximum number of pages to fetch when --paginate is set. Defaults to 1000. Use 0 for no limit (not recommended)
- `--preview` — Print the constructed request to stderr and exit without sending
- `--verbose, -v` — Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` — Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` — Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` — Profile name to use
- `--format, -F` — Output format
- `--no-color` — Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` — Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` — Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` — Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` — Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)
- `--retry-all-methods` — Retry all HTTP methods, not just GET/HEAD/OPTIONS. May cause duplicate writes on transient failures (a POST that creates a resource may run twice)

### atl auth

Manage authentication — login, logout, status, token

**Usage**

```
Usage: atl auth [OPTIONS] <COMMAND>
```

**Options**

- `--verbose, -v` — Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` — Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` — Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` — Profile name to use
- `--format, -F` — Output format
- `--no-color` — Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` — Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` — Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` — Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` — Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)
- `--retry-all-methods` — Retry all HTTP methods, not just GET/HEAD/OPTIONS. May cause duplicate writes on transient failures (a POST that creates a resource may run twice)

**Subcommands**

- `login` — Log in to Confluence or Jira and store the token in the OS keyring
- `logout` — Remove stored credentials for a profile/service
- `status` — Show which profiles/services are authenticated
- `token` — Print the resolved API token to stdout

#### atl auth login

Log in to Confluence or Jira and store the token in the OS keyring

**Usage**

```
Usage: atl auth login [OPTIONS]
```

**Options**

- `--service` — Service to log in to (defaults to both)
- `--profile` — Profile name (overrides the global --profile for this login)
- `--domain` — Atlassian domain (e.g. acme.atlassian.net). Prompted when omitted
- `--email` — Email address for Basic auth. Prompted when omitted and --auth-type=basic
- `--auth-type` — Authentication mechanism (basic = email + API token, bearer = PAT)
- `--with-token` — Read the token from stdin instead of prompting interactively
- `--skip-verify` — Skip the live verification request against the Atlassian API
- `--verbose, -v` — Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` — Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` — Path to configuration file
- `--format, -F` — Output format
- `--no-color` — Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` — Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` — Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` — Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` — Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)
- `--retry-all-methods` — Retry all HTTP methods, not just GET/HEAD/OPTIONS. May cause duplicate writes on transient failures (a POST that creates a resource may run twice)

#### atl auth logout

Remove stored credentials for a profile/service

**Usage**

```
Usage: atl auth logout [OPTIONS]
```

**Options**

- `--service` — Service to log out of (defaults to both)
- `--profile` — Profile name (overrides the global --profile for this logout)
- `--verbose, -v` — Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` — Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` — Path to configuration file
- `--format, -F` — Output format
- `--no-color` — Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` — Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` — Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` — Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` — Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)
- `--retry-all-methods` — Retry all HTTP methods, not just GET/HEAD/OPTIONS. May cause duplicate writes on transient failures (a POST that creates a resource may run twice)

Show which profiles/services are authenticated

```

**Options**

- `--profile` — Show status for this profile only (defaults to all)
- `--skip-verify` — Skip the live verification request against the Atlassian API
- `--verbose, -v` — Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` — Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` — Path to configuration file
- `--format, -F` — Output format
- `--no-color` — Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` — Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` — Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` — Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` — Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)
- `--retry-all-methods` — Retry all HTTP methods, not just GET/HEAD/OPTIONS. May cause duplicate writes on transient failures (a POST that creates a resource may run twice)

#### atl auth token

Print the resolved API token to stdout

**Usage**

```
Usage: atl auth token [OPTIONS]
```

**Options**

- `--service` — Which service's token to print (required)
- `--profile` — Profile name (overrides the global --profile)
- `--force` — Print the token even when stdout is a TTY
- `--verbose, -v` — Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` — Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` — Path to configuration file
- `--format, -F` — Output format
- `--no-color` — Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` — Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` — Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` — Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` — Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)
- `--retry-all-methods` — Retry all HTTP methods, not just GET/HEAD/OPTIONS. May cause duplicate writes on transient failures (a POST that creates a resource may run twice)
